### System Initializers for the Static Maps
### Part 1a: Specific System Initializers with pre-warp species - Early Space Age (Not used in Original Map)
### Part 1b: Specific System Initializers with pre-warp species - Atomic Age (Not used in Original Map)
### Part 1c: Specific System Initializers with pre-warp species - Machine Age and earlier (Not used in Original Map)
### Part 1d: Specific satellite initializers for Empire colonies (P'Jem; Kurill Prime)
### Part 2: Specific System Initializers with no pre-warp species (Not used in Original Map)
### Part 3: Specific System Initializers with no pre-warp species, and fewer colonizable planets (Used mainly in Original map, and to an extent in other maps.)
### Part 4: General System Initializers (Not used in Original Map)

@distance = 30
@base_moon_distance = 10

### Part 1a: Specific System Initializers with pre-warp species - Early Space Age

# Alpha Centauri
# Flavor, not a homeworld.
# There are multiple habitable planets in this system, due to the three stars.
# Alpha Centauri A has 13 planetoids, Alpha Centauri B had four planetoids before becoming a Red Giant due to a time destortion; Novel The Yesterday Saga by A.C. Crispin.
# Proxima Centauri has three planetoids and a major maintenance facility, DS9 Past Tense, Part I
# In TOS Alpha Centauri VII is a culture that was transported from 3rd BCE Greece
alpha_centauri_b = {
	name = "Alpha Centauri"	
	class = sc_g								
	planet = {		
		name = "Alpha Centauri A"
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0	
		orbit_angle = 1	
		size = 30	
		has_ring = no
	}
	planet = {
		class = "pc_b_class"

		orbit_angle = -30

	}
	planet = {
		class = "pc_gas_giant"

		orbit_angle = 125
		size = 31.84
		has_ring = yes
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance
		moon = {
			count = 4
			class = random_non_colonizable
			size = {min = 1 max = 7}
			orbit_distance = { min = 1 max = 5}
			orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 270}
		}
	}
	planet = {
		class = "pc_continental"
		orbit_distance = 30

	}

	planet = {
		name = "Al Rijil"
		class = "pc_continental"
		orbit_distance = 41						
		orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 270}					
		size = { min = 12 max = 14 }	
		tile_blockers = none
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			prevent_anomaly = yes
			# Early Space Age
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					create_species = {
						class = "CENTAUR"
						homeworld = THIS
						traits = { trait = "trait_quick_learners" trait = "trait_nomadic" }
					}
					create_country = {
						name = "Al Rijil"
						civics = { civic = civic_increasing_urbanization civic = civic_atmospheric_pollution }

							ethic = "ethic_xenophile"

						}
						type = primitive
					}
					last_created_country = {
						set_graphical_culture = industrial_01
						set_country_flag = early_space_age
						set_primitive_age = early_space_age
					}
					create_colony = {
						owner = last_created_country
						species = last_created
						ethos = owner
					}
					create_army = { owner = last_created species = last_created type = "postatomic_army" }
					create_army = { owner = last_created species = last_created type = "postatomic_army" }
					create_army = { owner = last_created species = last_created type = "postatomic_army" }
					create_army = { owner = last_created species = last_created type = "postatomic_army" }
					create_army = { owner = last_created species = last_created type = "postatomic_army" }
					create_fleet = { name = "Space Station" }
					last_created_fleet = {
						set_owner = last_created_country
						create_ship = { name = "Space Station" design = "Space Station" }

						limit = {
							has_blocker = no

						limit = {
							has_blocker = no
							has_grown_pop = no

						}
						create_pop = { species = last_created }

						limit = {
							has_blocker = no
							has_grown_pop = no
							has_growing_pop = no
						}
						create_pop = { species = last_created }

						limit = {
							has_blocker = no
							has_grown_pop = no
							has_growing_pop = no
						}
						create_pop = { species = last_created }

					random_tile = {
						limit = { 
							has_blocker = no 
							has_building = no 
							has_grown_pop = yes
						}
						set_building = "building_primitive_factory"
						add_deposit = d_mineral_deposit	
					}
					random_tile = {
						limit = { 
							has_blocker = no 
							has_building = no 
							has_grown_pop = yes
						}
						set_building = "building_primitive_factory"

						}

						add_deposit = d_engineering_deposit

						limit = { has_blocker = no has_building = no }

		name = "Achird"
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 30
		has_ring = no
		entity = "g_star_class_star_entity"
	}
	planet {
		name = "Eta Cassiopeiae B"
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 48
		orbit_angle = 90
		size = 30
		has_ring = no
		entity = "k_star_class_star_entity"
	}
	planet = {
		class = "pc_b_class"
		orbit_distance = 30
		orbit_angle = 30
		size = 8
		has_ring = no
	}
	planet = {
		class = "pc_toxic"
		orbit_distance = 12.8
		orbit_angle = 145
		size = 15
		has_ring = no
	}
	planet = {
		name = "Terra Nova"
		class = "pc_continental"
		orbit_distance = 31
		orbit_angle = 240
		size = { min = 15 max = 18 }
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			prevent_anomaly = yes
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = surface_impact
				days = -1
			}
			add_anomaly = STH_terra_nova_category
			random_tile = {
				limit = { has_building = no num_adjacent_tiles > 3 }
				remove_blocker = yes
			}
			random_tile = {
				limit = { has_blocker = yes }
				remove_blocker = yes
				set_blocker = tb_crater
				add_deposit = d_rich_mineral_deposit
				random_neighboring_tile = {
					remove_blocker = yes
					set_blocker = tb_radioactive_wasteland
					add_deposit = d_mineral_deposit
				}
				random_neighboring_tile = {
					remove_blocker = yes
					set_blocker = tb_radioactive_wasteland
					add_deposit = d_mineral_deposit
				}
			}
		}
		moon = {
			orbit_distance = 7
			class = "pc_barren_cold"
			size = {min = 3 max = 7}
			orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 270}
		}
		moon = {
			orbit_distance = 4
			class = "pc_barren_cold"
			size = {min = 1 max = 3}
			orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 270}
		}
	}
}

	planet = {

		class = rl_dry_planets
		size = 13
		orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 60 }
	}									
	change_orbit = 7
	planet = {									
		name = "Trappist-1g"
		class = rl_dry_planets		
		size = 18				
		orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 60 }
	}									
	change_orbit = 16
	planet = {									
		name = "Trappist-1h"
		class = rl_dry_planets		
		size = 16
		orbit_angle = { min = 30 max = 60 }
	}
	init_effect = {
		create_crystal_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_star = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = blue2_trigger_1
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_star = no
				NOT = {
					is_same_value = event_target:blue2_trigger_1
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = blue2_trigger_2
		}
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_star = no
				NOT = {
					is_same_value = event_target:blue2_trigger_1
					is_same_value = event_target:blue2_trigger_2
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = blue2_trigger_3
		}
		event_target:crystal_country = {

###	usage = misc_system_init
###	usage_odds = {
###		base = 4

###			factor = 0.1
###			NOT = { is_in_cluster = resource_cluster_1 }
###		}
###	}

# Cloud Entity
hs_08_b = {
	class = sc_b
	asteroids_distance = 95
	
	flags = { hostile_system void_system }
	
	planet = {
		count = 1
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = { min = 20 max = 30 }
		has_ring = no
	}
	
	change_orbit = 30
	
	planet = {
		count = 2
		orbit_distance = 20
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}
	
	change_orbit = 25
	
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 0 max 150 }
	}
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 160 max 330 }
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 2 max = 5 }
		orbit_distance = 25
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance
		
		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_cloud_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { is_star = yes }
			orbital_deposit_tile = {
				clear_deposits = yes
				add_deposit = d_rich_energy_deposit
			}
			event_target:cloud_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_modifier = cloud_power
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = cloud_power
						days = -1
					}
				}
				set_aggro_range = 500
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Void Cloud"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:cloud_country
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						set_location = PREVPREV
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
						set_aggro_range = 500
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Mining Drones
hs_12_b = {
	class = sc_m
	asteroids_distance = 95
	
	flags = { hostile_system drone_system_1 }
	
	planet = {
		count = 1
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = { min = 20 max = 30 }
		has_ring = no
	}
	
	change_orbit = 30
	
	planet = {
		count = 2
		orbit_distance = 20
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}
	
	change_orbit = 25
	
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 0 max 150 }
	}
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 160 max 330 }
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 2 max = 5 }
		orbit_distance = 25
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance
		
		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_drone_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station }
			orbital_deposit_tile = {
				clear_deposits = yes
				add_deposit = d_immense_mineral_deposit
			}
			event_target:drone_country = {
				save_event_target_as = mining_drones
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Ancient Mining Drones"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:drone_country
						while = {
							count = 10
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "Ancient Mining Drone"
							}
						}
						while = {
							count = 4
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "Ancient Combat Drone"
							}
						}
						set_location = PREVPREV
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
						set_aggro_range = 150
						queue_actions = {
							repeat = {
								wait = {
									duration = 999
									random = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_mining_station = {
				owner = event_target:mining_drones
			}
		}	
	}
}

			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_cloud_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { is_star = yes }
			orbital_deposit_tile = {
				clear_deposits = yes
				add_deposit = d_rich_energy_deposit
			}
			event_target:cloud_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_modifier = cloud_power
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = cloud_power
						days = -1
					}
				}
				set_aggro_range = 500
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Void Cloud"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:cloud_country
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = ""
							design = "Cloud Entity"
						}

					}
				}
				20 = {
					orbital_deposit_tile = {
						clear_deposits = yes
						add_deposit = d_immense_engineering_deposit
					}
				}
				10 = {
					orbital_deposit_tile = {
						clear_deposits = yes
						add_deposit = d_immense_society_deposit
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	change_orbit = 60

		count = 2
		class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
		orbit_distance = 20
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}
	
	change_orbit = 25
	
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 0 max 150 }
	}
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 160 max 330 }
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 2 max = 5 }
		class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
		orbit_distance = 25
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance
		
		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_drone_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station }
			orbital_deposit_tile = {
				clear_deposits = yes
				add_deposit = d_immense_mineral_deposit
			}
			event_target:drone_country = {
				save_event_target_as = mining_drones
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Ancient Mining Destroyers"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:drone_country
						while = {
							count = 30
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "Ancient Destroyer"
							}
						}
						set_location = PREVPREV
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
						set_aggro_range = 150
						queue_actions = {
							repeat = {
								wait = {
									duration = 999
									random = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_mining_station = {
				owner = event_target:mining_drones
			}
		}	
	}
}

			}
		}	
	}
}

# Mining Drone Destroyers
hsc_12_drone_destroyer_b = {
	class = rl_all_stars
	asteroids_distance = 125
	
	flags = { hostile_system drone_destroyer_system }
	
	planet = {
		count = 1
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = { min = 40 max = 60 }
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			random_list = {
				30 = {}
				40 = {
					orbital_deposit_tile = {
						clear_deposits = yes
						add_deposit = d_immense_physics_deposit
					}
				}
				20 = {
					orbital_deposit_tile = {
						clear_deposits = yes
						add_deposit = d_immense_engineering_deposit
					}
				}
				10 = {
					orbital_deposit_tile = {
						clear_deposits = yes
						add_deposit = d_immense_society_deposit
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	change_orbit = 60
	
	planet = {
		count = 2
		class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
		orbit_distance = 20
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}
	
	change_orbit = 25
	
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 0 max 150 }
	}
	planet = {
		class = random_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 160 max 330 }
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 2 max = 5 }
		class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
		orbit_distance = 25
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance
		
		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			class = "rl_unhabitable_planets"
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_drone_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station }
			orbital_deposit_tile = {
				clear_deposits = yes
				add_deposit = d_enormous1_mineral_deposit
			}
			event_target:drone_country = {
				save_event_target_as = mining_drones
				create_fleet = {
					name = "Asset Protection Unit"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:drone_country
						while = {
							count = 30
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "Ancient Destroyer"
							}
						}
						set_location = PREVPREV
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
						set_aggro_range = 150
						queue_actions = {
							repeat = {
								wait = {
									duration = 999
									random = 10
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_mining_station = {
				owner = event_target:mining_drones
			}
		}	
	}
}

hs_17_aclass_orion_b = {
	class = sc_a
	
	flags = { pirate_system pirate_2 }
	
	planet = {
		count = 1
		class = star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1

		has_ring = no
	}
	
	change_orbit = 45
	
	planet = {

		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		size = 25

		}

		class = star

		orbit_angle = 1

	}

		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
	}

		count = { min = 1 max = 2 }
		orbit_distance = 60
		class = pc_gas_giant
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		size = 25

			count = { min = 1 max = 4 }
			size = { min = 8 max = 20 }

		}
